It unzips multiple files simultaneously up to the limit of your CPU, memory, and disk drive performance to unzip files as quickly as possible. \r\n\r\nThere are now 2 ways to unzip files using this app:\r\n1.\tUnzip all files into the same directories as the zip files.\r\n        a.\tClick the Zip Files Folder Path Browse button and select a folder with one or more Zip files in it. \r\n        b.\tClick the Go button.\r\n        c.\tAll zip files in that folder and in any sub-folders of that folder will be unzipped in place. \r\n\r\n2.\tUnzip the files to an output folder.\r\n        a.\tClick the Zip Files Folder Path Browse button and select a folder with one or more Zip files in it. \r\n        b.\tClick the Output Folder Path Browse button and select the output folder.\r\n        c.\tClick the Go button.\r\n        d.\tAll zip files in that folder and in any sub-folders of that folder will be unzipped to the specified Output Folder. The zip files will remain in the Zip Files Folder. \r\n\r\nIf any errors occur during the unzip process, those errors will be written to a log file in the root of the specified Zip Files Folder. The log will be saved and opened for you to see to alert you that there may have been a problem.\r\n\r\nA help file is available in the app.\r\n\r\nNote: The application may be used with or without Internet.
